AssertionError: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
There is a known batch-variant accuracy issue with TP>=4 for both DTensor and Megatron backend.
See https://docs.nvidia.com/nemo/rl/latest/guides/dtensor-tp-accuracy.html#root-cause for more details.

Please choose either of the following solutions to avoid this issue:
1. Set tp_size to 1 or 2. (tensor_parallel_size for DTensor, or tensor_model_parallel_size for Megatron)
2. Set policy.train_micro_batch_size and policy.logprob_batch_size to be the same value.
3. Set loss_fn.force_on_policy_ratio=true to force ratio=1.0, this requires train_global_batch_size == num_prompts_per_step * num_generations_per_prompt.
4. Set NRL_IGNORE_TP_ACCURACY_CHECK=1 to bypass this check. (not recommended)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
There is a known batch-variant accuracy issue with TP>=4 for both DTensor and Megatron backend.
See https://docs.nvidia.com/nemo/rl/latest/guides/dtensor-tp-accuracy.html#root-cause for more details.

Please choose either of the following solutions to avoid this issue:

2. Set policy.train_micro_batch_size and policy.logprob_batch_size to be the same value.
